      <div class="container">
       <div class="text text-light">
        <h1 class="onload-sequential-fade">
         Explore the Mysteries of the Deep
        </h1>
        <p class="subhead onload-sequential-fade">
         The biggest aquarium in the western hemisphere just got a lot bigger. Our expansive new gallery, Sharks! Predators of the Deep, takes you from fear to fascination as you explore the epic views and experience unique encounters with our fierce new residents.
        </p>
        <a class="home-masthead-link no-autoscroll link onload-sequential-fade" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/sharks/">
         Explore the New Gallery
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="tickets-widget-wrap onload-sequential-fade">

       <div class="col right">
        <div class="slick animal-content">
         <header class="section-header">
          <h3 class="prehead">
           Encounters
          </h3>
          <h2 class="heading">
           Try the All-New, Immersive Shark &amp; Ray Interaction
          </h2>
          <p>
           Turn your fear into fascination. Suit up and get in the water with some of our sharks and rays in this newest animal interaction in our Sharks! Predators of the Deep gallery.
          </p>
          <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/experience/shark-ray-immersion/">
           Book Now
          </a>
         </header>
         <header class="section-header">
          <h3 class="prehead">
           Encounters
          </h3>
          <h2 class="heading">
           Get Up Close With a Sea Lion
          </h2>
          <p>
           Our unique Sea Lions Up Close program offers an exclusive, up close, and personal session with California sea lions in a safe, socially distant environment. You’ll learn more about these charismatic animals and the Aquarium’s rescue, research, and conservation initiatives. Plus, you'll get to watch a training session and get a socially distant selfie with a sea lion.
          </p>
          <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/experience/sea-lion-up-close-program/">
           Book Now
          </a>
         </header>
         <header class="section-header">
          <h3 class="prehead">
           Encounters
          </h3>
          <h2 class="heading">
           Suit Up &amp; Go For a Swim With Whale Sharks
          </h2>
          <p>
           Journey with Gentle Giants swim encounter is the only opportunity in the world where you are guaranteed to swim with whale sharks, manta rays, and more. You’ll get to swim with a snorkel in the Ocean Voyager exhibit, built by The Home Depot, with thousands of amazing animals for the experience of a lifetime.
          </p>
          <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/experience/journey-with-gentle-giants-swim/">
           Book Now
          </a>
         </header>
         <header class="section-header">
          <h3 class="prehead">
           Encounters
          </h3>
          <h2 class="heading">
           Get Ready to Cage Dive With Fearsome Sharks
          </h2>
          <p>
           This new animal interaction lets you submerge yourself in a shark enthusiast’s dream and venture into the deep with some of our predators of the deep. Take a ride through our new gallery and come face to face with a number of shark species, including the incredible great hammerhead and sand tiger sharks.
          </p>
          <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/experience/shark-cage-dive/">
           Book Now
          </a>
         </header>
         <header class="section-header">
          <h3 class="prehead">
           Encounters
          </h3>
          <h2 class="heading">
           Suit Up &amp; Scuba Dive With Whale Sharks
          </h2>
          <p>
           Journey with Gentle Giants dive encounter is the only opportunity in the world where you’re guaranteed to dive with whale sharks, manta rays, and thousands of other sea creatures. Suit up to SCUBA dive in the lively waters of the Ocean Voyager exhibit, and have the experience of a lifetime. (SCUBA certification required)
          </p>
          <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/experience/journey-with-gentle-giants-dive/">
           Book Now
          </a>
         </header>
        </div>

        <header>
         <h3>
          Whale Shark
         </h3>

          <i class="icon-cross">
          </i>
         </a>
        </header>
        <dl class="definitions">
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-latin">
          </i>
          Scientific Name
         </dd>
         <dt>
          <em>

         </dt>
         <dd>

         </dt>
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-info">
          </i>
          Fact

       <section class="animal-popover-content">
        <header>
         <h3>
          White Spotted Jelly
         </h3>
         <a class="close js-tippy-close">
          <i class="icon-cross">
          </i>
         </a>
        </header>
        <dl class="definitions">
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-latin">
          </i>
          Scientific Name
         </dd>
         <dt>
          <em>
           Phyllorhiza punctata
          </em>
         </dt>
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-conservation">
          </i>
          Conservation Status
         </dd>
         <dt>
          Not Evaluated
         </dt>
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-info">
          </i>
          Fact
         </dd>
         <dt>
          A large group of jellies is called a smack.
         </dt>
        </dl>
        <footer>
         <a class="button" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/animal/white-spotted-jelly/">

         </div>
         <div class="slider-text-left">
          <header>
           <h3 class="prehead">
            Research &amp; Conservation
           </h3>
           <h2 class="heading">
            African Penguins Are Officially Endangered
           </h2>
          </header>
          <div class="text">
           <p>
            African penguin population numbers have dropped 60% in the last 30 years. Georgia Aquarium aids in their fight for survival through breeding programs and partnerships with organizations in their native South Africa, like the South African Foundation for the Conservation of Coastal Birds.
           </p>
           <p>
            Find out what we're doing, how we're succeeding, and how you can support our mission.
           </p>
           <div class="buttons">
            <a class="button" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/african-penguin-research/" target="">
             Learn More
            </a>
            <a class="link" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/donations/" target="">
             Donate Now
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="right-content-wrap">
         <div class="content content-right">

          </div>

         <div class="slider-text-right">
          <header>
           <h3 class="prehead">
            How You Can Help
           </h3>
           <h2 class="heading">
            Become a Member to Help Us Make a Difference
           </h2>
          </header>
          <div class="text">
           <p>
            Georgia Aquarium membership supports not only African penguin survival but all of the Aquarium’s efforts in aquatic animal research and conservation. Membership and other contributions are critical to continuing our efforts and success in our mission.
           </p>
           <p>
            Members can take advantage of free general admission, plus discounts on special events, Aquarium programs, products, and more.
           </p>
           <div class="buttons">
            <a class="button" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/membership/" target="">

    <section aria-labeledby="section-id-7" class="content type-newsroom bg-color-gray" id="section-id-7" style="">
     <div class="container">
      <header>
       <h2 class="heading">
        What's New With the Aquarium
       </h2>
      </header>
      <ul class="news-stories">
       <li class="news-stories-item">

      <div class="popover js-scroll-to-kill" id="popover-lr-animal-fact-section-id-11">
       <section class="animal-popover-content">
        <header>
         <h3>
          Common Bottlenose Dolphin
         </h3>
         <a class="close js-tippy-close">
          <i class="icon-cross">
          </i>
         </a>
        </header>
        <dl class="definitions">
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-latin">
          </i>
          Scientific Name
         </dd>
         <dt>
          <em>
           Tursiops truncatus
          </em>
         </dt>
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-conservation">
          </i>
          Conservation Status
         </dd>
         <dt>
          Least Concern
         </dt>
         <dd>
          <i class="icon-info">
          </i>
          Fact
         </dd>
         <dt>
          Bottlenose dolphins shed their outer skin every 2 hours.
         </dt>
        </dl>
        <footer>
         <a class="button" href="https://www.georgiaaquarium.org/animal/bottlenose-dolphin/">
          See More Animal Facts
         </a>
        </footer>
       </section>

    </section>
